 ) Empty plastic bottles in railway stations and train coaches will now be the case of tomorrow, as the Railways are making T-shirts and caps from these empty plastic bottles of water

 The depositor of the plastic bottle will be given five rupees per bottle

 Reverse vending machines have been installed at four stations of East Central Railway at Patna Junction, Rajendranagar, Patna Sahib and Danapur station, crushing plastic bottles of water and making t-shirts and caps from it
 purv madhya railway ke mukhya jansampark adhikari (seepiaro) rajesh kumaar ne ieenes se kaha, "railway steshnon par bekaar pade rahane vaali khaali pani kii plastic botalon se purv madhya railway ab tii-shart bana rahi he
 The plastic from the bottle crusher machine installed at railway stations will be used to make T-shirts
 "unhone kaha, "ye tii-shart sabhi mausam main pahanane laayak hongi
 Railways has tied up with a Mumbai-based company to manufacture T-shirts

 He said, "according to an estimate, India consumes two to three percent of the plastic consumed in the world
 prati vyakti prati din plastic ausat khapat saat kilogram se aath kilogram he
